The humidor was meant for the boss to show off. No cigar supply at the place. Worst part: AC did not work - whatever setting you were using the room was always at moldy, stinking 24 degree Celsius, totally sticky with humidity. Clothes hangers were fixed with duct tape - this is what kind of hotel? Condoms next to cup ramen in the pantry cupboard, yummy. The breakfast included was mainly Chinese - Western style did not even include a reasonable coffee. In the restaurant all the plates were piled up on your table until you were finished - nobody bothered to clean up your table before you were done. Again, what kind of hotel is this and what kind of service would I expect? A lot more. Food is up to taste - I like Chinese food a lot, the Chinese food at the hotel, I did not like at all.

The riverside view was great, though and the room service and preparation was the best. I would rate it at 4.5/5. By contrast, the overall policy e.g. the no smoking situation ****** and advertised amenities did not exist any more or could not be used at all.

In conclusion to future trips to Wuzhou: I will not stay at this hotel again.
